
#### New Coalition stuff ####

startup_politics = {
	set_failsafe_values = yes #adds needed values if missing
	add_up_party_totals = yes
	set_party_positions = yes
	setup_election_threshold = yes #adds election_threshold if not set
	store_election_values = yes #add to election array
	update_majority_threshold = yes
	update_government_coalition_strength = yes
	update_party_name = yes
	reset_coalition_ideas = yes
	find_two_highest_parties = yes
}

start_politics_input = {
	clear_array = party_pop_array
	clear_array = party_pop_elect_array
	clear_array = pos_array
	clear_array = ruling_party
	clear_array = gov_coalition_array
	
	resize_array = { array = party_pop_array size = 24 }
	resize_array = { array = party_pop_elect_array size = 24 }
	resize_array = { array = pos_array size = 24 }
}

recalculate_party = {
	add_up_party_totals = yes
	set_party_positions = yes
	update_government_coalition_strength = yes
}


add_up_party_totals = {

	set_variable = { pop_total_democratic = 0 }
	set_variable = { pop_total_communism = 0 }
	set_variable = { pop_total_fascism = 0 }
	set_variable = { pop_total_neutrality = 0 }
	set_variable = { pop_total_nationalist = 0 }
	
	#sum of ideologies
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = party_pop_array^num
		set_variable = { current_id = v }
		meta_effect = {
			text = { add_to_variable = { pop_total_[PART_OF_IDEOLOGY1] = party_pop_array^v } }
			PART_OF_IDEOLOGY1 = "[offcial_name_party_ideology]"
		}
	}
	#Maintain consistency with outlooks
	for_loop_effect = {
        end = party_pop_array^num
        set_variable = { current_id = v }
        multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^v = 100 }
        meta_effect = {
            text = {
                divide_variable = { party_pop_array^v = pop_total_[PART_OF_IDEOLOGY2] }
                multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^v = party_popularity@[PART_OF_IDEOLOGY2] }
            }
            PART_OF_IDEOLOGY2 = "[offcial_name_party_ideology]"
        }
        round_variable = party_pop_array^v
        divide_variable = { party_pop_array^v = 100 }
    }
	clear_variable = current_id
}

set_party_positions = {
	resize_temp_array = { 
		array = party_pop_array_temp 
		size = 24
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = pos_array^num
		find_highest_in_array = {
			array = party_pop_array 
			value = max
			index = max_index
		}
		set_variable = { pos_array^v = max_index }
		set_variable = { party_pop_array^max_index = -1 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_pop_array_temp^max_index = max }
	}
	clear_array = party_pop_array
	for_each_loop = {
		array = party_pop_array_temp
		add_to_array = { party_pop_array = v  }
	}
	clear_temp_array = party_pop_array_temp
}

find_two_highest_parties = {
	find_highest_in_array = {
		array = party_pop_elect_array
		value = max_1_tmp
		index = max_index_1_tmp
	}
	set_variable = { max_index_1 = max_index_1_tmp }
	set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^max_index_1 = -1 }
	find_highest_in_array = {
		array = party_pop_elect_array
		value = max_2_tmp
		index = max_index_2_tmp
	}
	set_variable = { max_index_2 = max_index_2_tmp }
	set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^max_index_1 = max_1_tmp }
}

update_party_name = {
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = [OUTLOOK]
				name = [SUBIDEOLOGY_NAME]
				long_name = [SUBIDEOLOGY_NAME]
			}
		}
		OUTLOOK = "[meta_ideology_names]"
		SUBIDEOLOGY_NAME = "[show_ruling_party]"
	}
}

gov_pop_idea_add = {
	set_temp_variable = { add_t = government_coalition_differential }
	multiply_temp_variable = { add_t = 100 }
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			add_ideas = { 
				gov_pop_[POP_DIFF_ADD]
			}
		}
		POP_DIFF_ADD = "[?add_t|0]"
	}
}

gov_pop_idea_remove = {
	set_temp_variable = { remove_t = government_coalition_differential }
	multiply_temp_variable = { remove_t = 100 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			meta_trigger = {
				text = {
					has_idea = gov_pop_[POP_DIFF_HAS]
				}
				POP_DIFF_HAS = "[?remove_t|0]"
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				remove_ideas = { 
					gov_pop_[POP_DIFF_REMOVE]
				}
			}
			POP_DIFF_REMOVE = "[?remove_t|0]"
		}
	}
}

set_coalition_drift = {
	#reset coalition counts
	set_variable = { coalition_fascism = 0 }
	set_variable = { coalition_nationalist = 0 }
	set_variable = { coalition_communism = 0 }
	set_variable = { coalition_neutrality = 0 }
	set_variable = { coalition_democratic = 0 }
	clear_coalition_count_ideas = yes
	
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = 23 
		value = v
		set_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_elect_array^gov_coalition_array^v } #pop of current element
		set_temp_variable = { current_id = gov_coalition_array^v } #ID of current element
		
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				add_to_variable = { coalition_[PART_OF_IDEOLOGY] = sum }
			}
			PART_OF_IDEOLOGY = "[offcial_name_party_ideology]"
		}
	}
	#prevents adding to own ideology
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_variable = { coalition_[CURRENT_RULING_IDEOLOGY] = 0 }
		}
		CURRENT_RULING_IDEOLOGY = "[offcial_name_party_ideology]"
	}
	reset_democratic_coalition_ideas = yes
	reset_neutrality_coalition_ideas = yes
	reset_communism_coalition_ideas = yes
	reset_nationalist_coalition_ideas = yes
	reset_fascism_coalition_ideas = yes
}

update_government_coalition_strength = {
	gov_pop_idea_remove = yes #remove popularity idea
	set_temp_variable = { sum = 0 }
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = party_pop_array^num 
		value = v
		add_to_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_array^gov_coalition_array^v }
	}
	set_variable = { government_coalition_strength = sum }
	
	#strength of ruling_party is separate
	set_temp_variable = { sum = 0 }
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = ruling_party^num 
		value = v
		add_to_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_array^ruling_party^v }
	}
	add_to_variable = { government_coalition_strength = sum }
	
	### Now setup the election strength ###
	set_temp_variable = { sum = 0 }
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = party_pop_array^num 
		value = v
		add_to_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_elect_array^gov_coalition_array^v }
	}
	set_variable = { government_coalition_strength_elect = sum }
	
	#strength of ruling_party is separate
	set_temp_variable = { sum = 0 }
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = ruling_party^num 
		value = v
		add_to_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_elect_array^ruling_party^v }
	}
	add_to_variable = { government_coalition_strength_elect = sum }
	
	#find the differentials
	set_variable = { government_coalition_differential = government_coalition_strength }
	subtract_from_variable = { government_coalition_differential = government_coalition_strength_elect }
	#update_majority_threshold = yes
	gov_pop_idea_add = yes # give popularity idea
	set_coalition_drift = yes
	#find_two_highest_parties = yes
}

refund_government_coalition = {
	set_temp_variable = { sum_factor = 0 }
	for_loop_effect = {
		end = party_pop_array^num 
		value = v
		set_temp_variable = { sum = party_pop_elect_array^gov_coalition_array^v } #pop of current element
		set_temp_variable = { current_id = gov_coalition_array^v } #ID of current element
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				pol_distance_matrix_[NUM] = yes
			}
			NUM = "[?current_id|.0]"
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { sum = pol_distance_current }
		add_to_temp_variable = { sum_factor = sum }
	}
	set_variable = { pp_cost_to_invite = sum_factor }
	multiply_variable = { pp_cost_to_invite = 1500 } #75%
	add_political_power = pp_cost_to_invite
}

store_election_values = {

	for_loop_effect = {
		end = party_pop_array^num
		value = v
		if = {
			limit = {
				#if entry is 0 - true if no specific value has been set
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^v = 0 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {
					#entry is over threshold
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^v > election_threshold }
				}
				set_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^v = party_pop_array^v } #
			}
		}
	}
}

#only on startup
setup_election_threshold = {
	if = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = election_threshold } }
		set_variable = { election_threshold = 0.05 } #5% used as default
	}
}

#only needed for elections
update_majority_threshold = {
		set_temp_variable = { sum = 0 }
		for_each_loop = {
			array = party_pop_elect_array
			add_to_temp_variable = { sum = v }
		}
		set_variable = { majority_threshold = sum }
		divide_variable = { majority_threshold = 2 }
}

coalition_government_set_up = {
	recalculate_party = yes #in order to get the order of most recent list of popular parties
	clear_array = ruling_party
	clear_array = gov_coalition_array
	set_variable = { col_1_strength = 0 } #size of coalition 1 
	set_variable = { col_2_strength = 0 } #size of coalition 2
	
	coalition_leaders_setup = yes
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { col_1_strength > majority_threshold } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { col_2_strength > majority_threshold } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { conservatism_position = 3 }
			}
			coalition_conservatism_preference = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { liberalism_position = 3 }
			}
			coalition_liberalism_preference = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { socialism_position = 3 }
			}
			coalition_socialism_preference = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Western_Autocracy_position = 3 }
			}
			coalition_Western_Autocracy_preference = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Communist-State_position = 3 }
			}
			coalition_Communist-State_preference = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Conservative_position = 3 }
			}
			coalition_Conservative_preference = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Autocracy_position = 3 }
			}
			coalition_Autocracy_preference = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Vilayat_e_Faqih_position = 3 }
			}
			coalition_Vilayat_e_Faqih_preference = yes

		limit = { has_country_flag = col_1_member_Monarchist }
		clr_country_flag = col_1_member_Monarchist
	}
}

coalition_leaders_setup = {
	#These set the party leader for the first coalition
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { conservatism_position = 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_leader_conservatism
		set_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { liberalism_position = 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_leader_liberalism
		set_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { socialism_position = 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_leader_socialism
		set_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Western_Autocracy_position = 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_leader_Western_Autocracy
		set_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Communist-State_position = 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_leader_Communist-State
		set_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^4 }

coalition_conservatism_preference = {
	#Non Aligned Conservative
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_1_leader_Neutral_conservatism
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_member_conservatism
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_2_leader_Neutral_conservatism
		}
		set_country_flag = col_2_member_conservatism
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_2_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	
	#Libertarian
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_1_leader_Neutral_Libertarian
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_member_conservatism
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_2_leader_Neutral_Libertarian
		}
		set_country_flag = col_2_member_conservatism
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_2_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	
	#Prowestern Autocrat
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_1_leader_Western_Autocracy
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_member_conservatism
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_2_leader_Western_Autocracy
		}
		set_country_flag = col_2_member_conservatism
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_2_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	
	#Reactionary
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_1_leader_Conservative
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_member_conservatism
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_2_leader_Conservative
		}
		set_country_flag = col_2_member_conservatism
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_2_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	
	#Fascist
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_1_leader_Nat_Fascism
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_member_conservatism
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_2_leader_Nat_Fascism
		}
		set_country_flag = col_2_member_conservatism
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_2_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	
	#Non Aligned Autocrat
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_1_leader_Neutral_Autocracy
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_member_conservatism
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^1 }
	}
	if = {

		set_country_flag = col_1_member_Monarchist
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^23 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_2_leader_conservatism
		}
		set_country_flag = col_2_member_Monarchist
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_2_strength = party_pop_array^23 }
	}
	
	#Liberal
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_1_leader_liberalism
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_member_Monarchist
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^23 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_2_leader_liberalism
		}
		set_country_flag = col_2_member_Monarchist
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_2_strength = party_pop_array^23 }
	}
	
	#Non Aligned Communist

		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_1_leader_Neutral_Communism
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_member_Monarchist
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^23 }
	}

			has_country_flag = col_2_leader_Neutral_Communism
		}
		set_country_flag = col_2_member_Monarchist
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_2_strength = party_pop_array^23 }
	}
	
	#Reactionary

		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_1_leader_Conservative
		}
		set_country_flag = col_1_member_Monarchist
		set_country_flag = found_member
		add_to_variable = { col_1_strength = party_pop_array^23 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = found_member }
			has_country_flag = col_2_leader_Conservative
		}
		set_country_flag = col_2_member_Monarchist
		set_country_flag = found_member

##Western_Autocracy
pol_distance_matrix_0 = { 
	if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } } #conservatism
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.2 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } } #liberalism
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.4 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 } } #socialism
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.4 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } } #Communist-State
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } } #anarchist_communism

			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.4 }
	}

			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.5 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 8 } } #Mod_Vilayat_e_Faqih
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }

	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 11 } } #Caliphate

	}

	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 } } #oligarchism

	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 12 } } #Neutral_Muslim_Brotherhood
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 } } #Neutral_Autocracy
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.4 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 } } #Neutral_conservatism
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.9 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 } } #oligarchism
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.8 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 } } #Neutral_Libertarian
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 } } #Neutral_green
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 } } #neutral_Social
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 1 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } } #Neutral_Communism
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.9 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } } #Nat_Populism
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.4 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } } #Nat_Fascism
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.4 }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } } #Nat_Autocracy
			set_variable = { pol_distance_current = 0.2 }
	}
}
